(**********************************************************************************

 Composing a two-sided displayed category with a displayed category

 We show how to compose a two-sided displayed category with a displayed category.
 The idea is basically as follows: a two-sided displayed category represents a
 span and a displayed category represents a functor. Both legs of the span get
 composed with this functor to obtain a new span.

 More precisely, we have a two-sided displayed category and a displayed category
 over the total category of that two-sided displayed category. This displayed
 category represents structures/properties to be added to our two-sided displayed
 category. We then form a new two-sided displayed category by taking sigma-types.

 Contents
 1. The definition
 2. Isomorphisms
 3. Univalence and discreteness

 **********************************************************************************)

Local Open Scope cat.


X: UU
Y: X → UU
Xisaset: isaset X
x₁, x₂: X
p, q: x₁ = x₂
y: Y x₁
transportf Y p y = transportf Y q y


X: UU
Y: X → UU
Xisaset: isaset X
x₁, x₂: X
p, q: x₁ = x₂
y: Y x₁
transportf Y p y = transportf Y q y

  
X: UU
Y: X → UU
Xisaset: isaset X
x₁, x₂: X
p, q: x₁ = x₂
y: Y x₁
p = q

  apply Xisaset.
Qed.

Section DispCatOnTwoSidedDispCat.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : category}
          (D₁ : twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂)
          (D₂ : disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)).

   1. The definition

twosided_disp_cat_ob_mor C₁ C₂

C₁ → C₂ → UU
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
(λ D : C₁ → C₂ → UU,
 ∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
 D x₁ y₁
 → D x₂ y₂ → C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧ → C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧ → UU) ?pr1

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
C₁ → C₂ → UU
 exact (λ x y, ∑ (xy : D₁ x y), D₂ (x ,, y ,, xy)).
    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
(λ D : C₁ → C₂ → UU,
 ∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
 D x₁ y₁
 → D x₂ y₂ → C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧ → C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧ → UU)
  (λ (x : C₁) (y : C₂), ∑ xy : D₁ x y, D₂ (x,, y,, xy))
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ xy₁ xy₂ f g,
             ∑ (fg : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g ] pr1 xy₂),
             pr2 xy₁ -->[ f ,, g ,, fg ] pr2 xy₂).
  Defined.

C₁, C₂: category

D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_ob_mor x y
(λ fg : pr1 xy -->[ identity x ][ identity y] pr1 xy,
 pr2 xy -->[ identity x,, identity y,, fg] pr2 xy)
  (id_two_disp (pr1 xy))

      apply (@id_disp (total_twosided_disp_category D₁) D₂).
    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
(λ _ : twosided_disp_cat_id
         sigma_twosided_disp_cat_ob_mor,
 twosided_disp_cat_comp sigma_twosided_disp_cat_ob_mor)
  (λ (x : C₁) (y : C₂)
   (xy : sigma_twosided_disp_cat_ob_mor x y),
   id_two_disp (pr1 xy),, id_disp (pr2 xy))
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ x₃ y₁ y₂ y₃ xy₁ xy₂ xy₃ f₁ f₂ g₁ g₂ fg₁ fg₂,
             pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂
             ,,
             (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂)%mor_disp).
  Defined.

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg₁, fg₂: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
p: pr1 fg₁ = pr1 fg₂
q: transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) p) (pr2 fg₁) = pr2 fg₂
fg₁ = fg₂

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg₁, fg₂: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
p: pr1 fg₁ = pr1 fg₂
q: transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) p) (pr2 fg₁) = pr2 fg₂
fg₁ = fg₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
fg₂: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
p: pr1 (fg₁,, fg₁') = pr1 fg₂
q: transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, 
         x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) p) (pr2 (fg₁,, fg₁')) = 
pr2 fg₂
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
fg₂: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₂': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₂] pr2 xy₂
p: pr1 (fg₁,, fg₁') = pr1 (fg₂,, fg₂')
q: transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, 
         x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) p) (pr2 (fg₁,, fg₁')) =
pr2 (fg₂,, fg₂')
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₂,, fg₂'

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: ∑ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)
xy₂: ∑ xy : D₁ x₂ y₂, D₂ (x₂,, y₂,, xy)
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
fg₂: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₂': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₂] pr2 xy₂
p: fg₁ = fg₂
q: transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
         (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) p) fg₁' = fg₂'
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₂,, fg₂'

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: ∑ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)
xy₂: ∑ xy : D₁ x₂ y₂, D₂ (x₂,, y₂,, xy)
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁', fg₂': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
q: transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
         (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      f,, g,, z) (idpath fg₁)) fg₁' = fg₂'
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₁,, fg₂'

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: ∑ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)
xy₂: ∑ xy : D₁ x₂ y₂, D₂ (x₂,, y₂,, xy)
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁', fg₂': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
q: fg₁' = fg₂'
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₁,, fg₂'

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: ∑ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)
xy₂: ∑ xy : D₁ x₂ y₂, D₂ (x₂,, y₂,, xy)
fg₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂
fg₁': pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, fg₁] pr2 xy₂
fg₁,, fg₁' = fg₁,, fg₁'

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Section SigmaLeft.
    Context {x₁ x₂ : C₁}
            {f : x₁ --> x₂}
            {y₁ y₂ : C₂}
            {g₁ g₂ : y₁ --> y₂}
            (p : g₂ = g₁)
            {xy₁ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁}
            {xy₂ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂}
            (fg : xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂ ] xy₂).

    Let q₁ : total_twosided_disp_category D₁ := x₁ ,, y₁ ,, pr1 xy₁.
    Let q₂ : total_twosided_disp_category D₁ := x₂ ,, y₂ ,, pr1 xy₂.
    Let h₁ : q₁ --> q₂ := f ,, g₂ ,, pr1 fg.
    Let h₂ : q₁ --> q₂ := f ,, g₁ ,, transportf (λ z, _ -->[ f ][ z ] _) p (pr1 fg).

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₁, g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
p: g₂ = g₁
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f,, g₂,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f,,
g₁,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) p (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₁, g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
p: g₂ = g₁
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f,, g₂,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f,,
g₁,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) p (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
p: g₂ = g₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f,, g₂,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f,,
g₂,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (idpath g₂)
  (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

      apply idpath.
    Defined.
  End SigmaLeft.

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₁, g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
p: g₂ = g₁
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] xy₂)
  p fg =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
  p (pr1 fg),,
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_left_path p fg) (pr2 fg)

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₁, g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
p: g₂ = g₁
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] xy₂)
  p fg =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
  p (pr1 fg),,
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_left_path p fg) (pr2 fg)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
y₁, y₂: C₂
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g₂] xy₂
fg = pr1 fg,, pr2 fg

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Section SigmaRight.
    Context {x₁ x₂ : C₁}
            {f₁ f₂ : x₁ --> x₂}
            (p : f₂ = f₁)
            {y₁ y₂ : C₂}
            {g : y₁ --> y₂}
            {xy₁ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁}
            {xy₂ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂}
            (fg : xy₁ -->[ f₂ ][ g ] xy₂).

    Let q₁ : total_twosided_disp_category D₁ := x₁ ,, y₁ ,, pr1 xy₁.
    Let q₂ : total_twosided_disp_category D₁ := x₂ ,, y₂ ,, pr1 xy₂.
    Let h₁ : q₁ --> q₂ := f₂ ,, g ,, pr1 fg.
    Let h₂ : q₁ --> q₂ := f₁ ,, g ,, transportf (λ z, _ -->[ z ][ g ] _) p (pr1 fg).

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f₁, f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
p: f₂ = f₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f₂ ][ g] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f₂,, g,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f₁,,
g,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g] pr1 xy₂) p (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f₁, f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
p: f₂ = f₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f₂ ][ g] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f₂,, g,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f₁,,
g,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g] pr1 xy₂) p (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
p: f₂ = f₂
y₁, y₂: C₂
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
fg: xy₁ -->[ f₂ ][ g] xy₂
q₁:= x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
q₂:= x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂: total_twosided_disp_category D₁
h₁:= f₂,, g,, pr1 fg: total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₂:= f₂,,
g,,
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g] pr1 xy₂) (idpath f₂)
  (pr1 fg): total_twosided_disp_category D₁ ⟦ q₁, q₂ ⟧
h₁ = h₂

      apply idpath.
    Defined.
  End SigmaRight.

C₁, C₂: category

f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg = trb₂ fg

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] xy₂) (! id_left f)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] xy₂)
     (! id_left g) fg)

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] xy₂) (! id_left f)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_left g)
     (pr1 fg),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂)
  (! id_left f)
  (pr1
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_left g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg))),,
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_left g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (pr2
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_left g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg) =
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂)
     (! id_left f)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg)))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))))
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x₁ · f
            ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x₁ · f,, identity y₁ · g,, z) ?p)
  (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg)) =
pr2
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂)
     (! id_left f)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg)))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))))

      
C₁, C₂: category

x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg) =
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂)
     (! id_left f)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg)))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))))
 apply id_two_disp_left.
      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x₁ · f
            ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x₁ · f,, identity y₁ · g,, z)
     (id_two_disp_left (pr1 fg)))
  (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁ ;;2 fg)) =
pr2
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂)
     (! id_left f)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg)))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))))
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x₁ · f
            ][ identity y₁ · g] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x₁ · f,, identity y₁ · g,, z)
     (id_two_disp_left (pr1 fg)))
  (id_disp (pr2 xy₁) ;; pr2 fg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_left g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
         pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
              (identity x₁ · f) (identity y₁ · g),
      identity x₁ · f,, identity y₁ · g,, z)
     (id_two_disp_left (pr1 fg)))
  (id_disp (pr2 xy₁) ;; pr2 fg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_left f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)
        (! id_left g) (pr1 fg),,

        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)

                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,

     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,

                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_left g) fg)

f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
isaset
  (total_twosided_disp_precategory_ob_mor D₁
   ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧)

        apply (total_twosided_disp_category D₁).
    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
id_two_disp_right_law sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
fg ;;2 id_two_disp xy₂ = trb₂ fg

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
fg ;;2 id_two_disp xy₂ =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ g · identity y₂] xy₂) (! id_right f)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] xy₂)
     (! id_right g) fg)

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂

g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
fg ;;2 id_two_disp xy₂ =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ g · identity y₂] xy₂) (! id_right f)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_right g)
     (pr1 fg),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

  (pr1
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_right g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg))),,
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_right g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (pr2
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_right g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f · identity x₂
            ][ g · identity y₂] pr1 xy₂,
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg)))
  (pr2 (fg ;;2 id_two_disp xy₂)) =
pr2
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g · identity y₂] pr1 xy₂)
     (! id_right f)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g)
              fg) (pr2 fg))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂)
           (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f · identity x₂
            ][ g · identity y₂] pr1 xy₂,
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg)))
  (pr2 fg ;; id_disp (pr2 xy₂))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ z] pr1 xy₂) (! id_right g)
        (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
         pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
              (f · identity x₂) (g · identity y₂),
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg)))
  (pr2 fg ;; id_disp (pr2 xy₂))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)
        (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
              (f · identity x₂) (g · identity y₂),
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg)))
  (pr2 fg ;; id_disp (pr2 xy₂))%mor_disp = ?b
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
?b =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)
        (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
              (f · identity x₂) (g · identity y₂),
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg)))
  (transportb (mor_disp (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂))
     (id_right (f,, g,, pr1 fg)) (pr2 fg)) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)
        (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg)))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
     (pr2 fg))

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

  (transportf (mor_disp (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂))
     (! id_right (f,, g,, pr1 fg)) (pr2 fg)) =

  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)

            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (! id_right (f,, g,, pr1 fg) @
   maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
              (f · identity x₂) (g · identity y₂),
      f · identity x₂,, g · identity y₂,, z)
     (id_two_disp_right (pr1 fg))) (pr2 fg) =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg @
   sigma_transportf_right_path (! id_right f)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f z)
        (! id_right g) (pr1 fg),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
               pr2 D₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)
                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! id_right g) fg)
        (pr2 fg))) (pr2 fg)

D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

isaset
  (total_twosided_disp_precategory_ob_mor D₁
   ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧)

        apply (total_twosided_disp_category D₁).

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
fg₁ ;;2 (fg₂ ;;2 fg₃) = trb₂ (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
fg₁ ;;2 (fg₂ ;;2 fg₃) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)] xy₄)
  (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
      xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] xy₄)
     (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
fg₁ ;;2 (fg₂ ;;2 fg₃) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧,
   xy₁ -->[ z ][ g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)] xy₄)
  (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
     (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
        (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
     (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
fg₁ ;;2 (fg₂ ;;2 fg₃) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)] pr1 xy₄)
  (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
  (pr1
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
        (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
        (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)))),,
transportf
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
        (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
        (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))))
  (pr2
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
        (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄
               ⟧, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
        (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))))

x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁

xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧

g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 (fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)) =
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)] pr1 xy₄)
     (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
           (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path
              (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
           (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁, x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
           (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁,
                  x₄,, y₄,, pr1 xy₄ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path
              (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
           (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
           (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (pr1 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)),,

              (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃))
           (pr2 (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂ ;;2 fg₃)))))

x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₄,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · (f₂ · f₃)
            ][ g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)] pr1 xy₄,
      f₁ · (f₂ · f₃),, g₁ · (g₂ · g₃),, z)
     (assoc_two_disp (pr1 fg₁) (pr1 fg₂) (pr1 fg₃)))
  (pr2 fg₁ ;; (pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₄,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f₁ · f₂ · f₃ ][ z] pr1 xy₄)
        (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
        (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
               pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₄,
         pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃,,
            (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
        (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₄,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
        (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃,,
         (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
     (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp)

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
xy₃: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₃ y₃
xy₄: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₄ y₄
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: C₁ ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: C₂ ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ -->[ f₃ ][ g₃] xy₄
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄)
              (f₁ · (f₂ · f₃)) (g₁ · (g₂ · g₃)),
      f₁ · (f₂ · f₃),, g₁ · (g₂ · g₃),, z)
     (assoc_two_disp (pr1 fg₁) (pr1 fg₂) (pr1 fg₃)))
  (pr2 fg₁ ;; (pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄) f g,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
  (sigma_transportf_right_path (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧,
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄)
           (f₁ · f₂ · f₃) z) (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
        (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃),,
      transportf
        (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧)
               (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
               pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄)
                 f g, pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
           (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃,,
            (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
        (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
  (transportf
     (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
            pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄) f g,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₄)
     (sigma_transportf_left_path (! assoc g₁ g₂ g₃)
        (pr1 fg₁ ;;2 pr1 fg₂ ;;2 pr1 fg₃,,
         (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))
     (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp)

  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧),
         pr2 D₁ x₁ x₄ y₁ y₄ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₄) f g,

      f₁ · (f₂ · f₃),, g₁ · (g₂ · g₃),, z)

            (pr2 fg₁ ;; pr2 fg₂ ;; pr2 fg₃)%mor_disp))

xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
isaset (xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂)

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧
fg₁, fg₂: xy -->[ f ][ g] xy
p: fg₁ = fg₂
pr2 fg₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy, x,, y,, pr1 xy ⟧,
   pr2 xy -->[ z] pr2 xy)
  (maponpaths
     (tpair
        (λ f : C₁ ⟦ pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
               pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         ∑
         g : C₂ ⟦ pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
             pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) -->[ f
         ][ g] pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy)) f)
     (maponpaths
        (λ z : pr1 xy -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy, g,, z)
        (maponpaths pr1 p))) (pr2 fg₂)

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧
fg₁, fg₂: xy -->[ f ][ g] xy
p: fg₁ = fg₂
pr2 fg₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy, x,, y,, pr1 xy ⟧,
   pr2 xy -->[ z] pr2 xy)
  (maponpaths
     (tpair
        (λ f : C₁ ⟦ pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
               pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         ∑
         g : C₂ ⟦ pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
             pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) -->[ f
         ][ g] pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy)) f)
     (maponpaths
        (λ z : pr1 xy -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy, g,, z)
        (maponpaths pr1 p))) (pr2 fg₂)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)

f: C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧
fg₁: xy -->[ f ][ g] xy
pr2 fg₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy, x,, y,, pr1 xy ⟧,
   pr2 xy -->[ z] pr2 xy)
  (maponpaths
     (tpair
        (λ f : C₁ ⟦ pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
               pr1 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         ∑
         g : C₂ ⟦ pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy),
             pr12 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) ⟧,
         pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy) -->[ f
         ][ g] pr22 (x,, y,, pr1 xy)) f)
     (maponpaths
        (λ z : pr1 xy -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy, g,, z)
        (maponpaths pr1 (idpath fg₁)))) (pr2 fg₁)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂

(pr1 f,, pr1 g) ;;2 (pr12 f,,
                     inv_mor_disp_from_z_iso g) =
trb₂ id_two_disp xy₁
 abstract
        (unfold transportb_disp_mor2, transportf_disp_mor2 ;
         rewrite sigma_transportf_left ;
         rewrite sigma_transportf_right ;
         use sigma_twosided_disp_cat_mor_eq ; [ exact (pr122 f) | ] ;
         etrans ;
         [ apply maponpaths ;
           exact (inv_mor_after_z_iso_disp g)
         | ] ;
         unfold transportb ; cbn ;
         rewrite !transport_f_f ;
         apply transportf_hset_eq ;
         apply (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)).

                            inv_mor_disp_from_z_iso g) =
       trb₂ id_two_disp xy₁,
 (pr12 f,, inv_mor_disp_from_z_iso g) ;;2 (pr1 f,,
                                           pr1 g) =
 trb₂ id_two_disp xy₂)
  (to_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_subproof x y xy₁
     xy₂ f g)
 abstract
        (unfold transportb_disp_mor2, transportf_disp_mor2 ;
         rewrite sigma_transportf_left ;
         rewrite sigma_transportf_right ;
         use sigma_twosided_disp_cat_mor_eq ; [ exact (pr222 f) | ] ;
         etrans ;
         [ apply maponpaths ;
           exact (z_iso_disp_after_inv_mor g)
         | ] ;
         unfold transportb ; cbn ;
         rewrite !transport_f_f ;
         apply transportf_hset_eq ;
         apply (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)).
  Defined.

  Section FromSigmaIso.
    Context {x : C₁}
            {y : C₂}
            {xy₁ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y}
            {xy₂ : sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y}
            (f : @iso_twosided_disp
                    _ _
                    sigma_twosided_disp_cat
                    _ _ _ _
                    (identity_z_iso x)
                    (identity_z_iso y)
                    xy₁
                    xy₂).

    Let h : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x ][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂ := pr11 f.
    Let hinv : pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x ][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁ := pr112 f.

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
h ;;2 hinv =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
h ;;2 hinv =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
pr1 (trb₂ id_two_disp xy₁) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
      xy₁ -->[ z
      ][ (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
          pr2 (identity_z_iso y))
         · inv_from_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso y))] xy₁)
     (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
          (pr1 (identity_z_iso x),,
           pr2 (identity_z_iso x)))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
         xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] xy₁)
        (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
        (id_two_disp xy₁))) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
      xy₁ -->[ z
      ][ (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
          pr2 (identity_z_iso y))
         · inv_from_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso y))] xy₁)
     (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
          (pr1 (identity_z_iso x),,
           pr2 (identity_z_iso x)))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
        (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
        (pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁)),,
      transportf
        (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
               ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₁ ⟧,
         pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₁)
        (sigma_transportf_left_path
           (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                 pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
           (id_two_disp xy₁)) (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁)))) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
f: iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
  (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂
h:= pr11 f: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₂
hinv:= pr112 f: pr1 xy₂ -->[ identity_z_iso x
][ identity_z_iso y] pr1 xy₁
pr1
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ z
      ][ (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
          pr2 (identity_z_iso y))
         · inv_from_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso y))] pr1 xy₁)
     (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
          (pr1 (identity_z_iso x),,
           pr2 (identity_z_iso x)))
     (pr1
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
           (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                 pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
           (pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁)),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₁ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₁)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path
              (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                   (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                    pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
              (id_two_disp xy₁))
           (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁)))),,
   transportf
     (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
            ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₁ ⟧,
      pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₁)
     (sigma_transportf_right_path
        (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
             (pr1 (identity_z_iso x),,
              pr2 (identity_z_iso x)))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
           (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                 pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
           (pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁)),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₁ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₁)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path
              (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                   (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                    pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
              (id_two_disp xy₁))
           (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁))))
     (pr2
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
            pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
           (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                 pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
           (pr1 (id_two_disp xy₁)),,
         transportf
           (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
                  ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₁ ⟧,
            pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₁)
           (sigma_transportf_left_path
              (! z_iso_inv_after_z_iso
                   (pr1 (identity_z_iso y),,
                    pr2 (identity_z_iso y)))
              (id_two_disp xy₁))
           (pr2 (id_two_disp xy₁))))) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   pr1 xy₁ -->[ z ][ identity y · identity y] pr1 xy₁)
  (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso x))
  (transportb
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧,
      pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ z] pr1 xy₁)
     (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso (identity_z_iso y))
     (id_two_disp (pr1 xy₁)))

      apply idpath.
    Qed.

xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
h₁, h₂: ∑
f : iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
      (identity_z_iso y) (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂),
z_iso_disp
  (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁ f)
  (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂)
p: pr11 h₁ = pr11 h₂
q: pr12 h₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x
            ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x,, identity y,, z) p) (pr12 h₂)
h₁ = h₂

transportb
  (λ z : total_twosided_disp_category D₁
         ⟦ x,, y,, pr1 xy₁, x,, y,, pr1 xy₂ ⟧,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x
            ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x,, identity y,, z) p)
  (pr12 ((h₂,, Hh₂),, k₂,, Hk₂))
(h₁,, Hh₁),, k₁,, Hk₁ = (h₂,, Hh₂),, k₂,, Hk₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
x: C₁
y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: ∑ xy : D₁ x y, D₂ (x,, y,, xy)
h₁: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂
Hh₁: is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso x) (identity_is_z_iso y) h₁
k₁: pr2 xy₁ -->[
identity x,, identity y,, h₁] pr2 xy₂
Hk₁: is_z_iso_disp (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁ (h₁,, Hh₁)) k₁
h₂: pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂
Hh₂: is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso x) (identity_is_z_iso y) h₂
k₂: pr2 xy₁ -->[
identity x,, identity y,, h₂] pr2 xy₂
Hk₂: is_z_iso_disp (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁ (h₂,, Hh₂)) k₂
p: h₁ = h₂
q: k₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x
            ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x,, identity y,, z) p) k₂
(h₁,, Hh₁),, k₁,, Hk₁ = (h₂,, Hh₂),, k₂,, Hk₂

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

Hh₂: is_iso_twosided_disp (identity_is_z_iso x) (identity_is_z_iso y) h₁
k₂: pr2 xy₁ -->[
identity x,, identity y,, h₁] pr2 xy₂
Hk₂: is_z_iso_disp (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁ (h₁,, Hh₂)) k₂
q: k₁ =
transportb
  (λ z : ∑ (f : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧) (g : C₂ ⟦ y, y ⟧),
         pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ z] pr2 xy₂)
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 xy₁ -->[ identity x
            ][ identity y] pr1 xy₂,
      identity x,, identity y,, z) (idpath h₁)) k₂
(h₁,, Hh₁),, k₁,, Hk₁ = (h₁,, Hh₂),, k₂,, Hk₂

y: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x y
(∑
 f : iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
       (identity_z_iso y) (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂),
 z_iso_disp (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁ f)
   (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂))
≃ iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
    (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂

 to_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat (pr1 f) (pr2 f))
  ((λ f : iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x)
            (identity_z_iso y) xy₁ xy₂,
    from_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_pr1 f,,
    from_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_pr2 f) y0) =
y0
 abstract
        (intro f ;
         use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isaprop_is_iso_twosided_disp | ] ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

  (**
   3. Univalence and discreteness
   *)
  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
p: pr1 xy₁ = pr1 xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : (λ y : C₂, D₁ x₁ y) y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z)) p
  (pr2 xy₁) = pr2 xy₂
≃ z_iso_disp
    (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
       (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
          p)) (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂)

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
p: pr1 xy₁ = pr1 xy₂
transportf
  (λ z : (λ y : C₂, D₁ x₁ y) y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z)) p
  (pr2 xy₁) = pr2 xy₂
≃ z_iso_disp
    (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
       (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
          p)) (pr2 xy₁) (pr2 xy₂)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁

z₁: D₁ x₁ y₁
z₂: D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z₁)
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
p: pr1 (z₁,, z₂) = pr1 xy₂
transportf (λ z : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z)) p
  (pr2 (z₁,, z₂)) = pr2 xy₂
≃ z_iso_disp
    (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
       (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
          p)) (pr2 (z₁,, z₂)) (pr2 xy₂)

D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

z₂: D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z₁)
z₃: D₁ x₁ y₁
z₄: D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z₃)
p: pr1 (z₁,, z₂) = pr1 (z₃,, z₄)
transportf (λ z : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z)) p
  (pr2 (z₁,, z₂)) = pr2 (z₃,, z₄)
≃ z_iso_disp
    (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
       (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
          p)) (pr2 (z₁,, z₂)) (pr2 (z₃,, z₄))

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
z₁: D₁ x₁ y₁
z₂: D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z₁)
z₃: D₁ x₁ y₁
z₄: D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z₃)
p: z₁ = z₃
transportf (λ z : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, z)) p z₂ =
z₄
≃ z_iso_disp
    (make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
       (paths_rect (D₁ x₁ y₁) z₁
          (λ (xy₂ : D₁ x₁ y₁) (_ : z₁ = xy₂),
           iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x₁)
             (identity_z_iso y₁) z₁ xy₂)
          (id_iso_twosided_disp z₁) z₃ p)) z₂ z₄

x₁: C₁

xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
transportf (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
  (idpath x₁)
  (transportf (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
     (idpath y₁) xy₁) = xy₂
≃ iso_twosided_disp (idtoiso (idpath x₁))
    (idtoiso (idpath y₁)) xy₁ xy₂
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: is_univalent_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
?w ~ idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: is_univalent_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
transportf (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
  (idpath x₁)
  (transportf (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
     (idpath y₁) xy₁) = xy₂
≃ iso_twosided_disp (idtoiso (idpath x₁))
    (idtoiso (idpath y₁)) xy₁ xy₂
 exact (weq_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat _ _
             ∘ weqtotal2
                 (make_weq _ (HD₁ x₁ x₁ y₁ y₁ (idpath _) (idpath _) (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)))
                 (is_univalent_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_help HD₂ xy₁ xy₂)
             ∘ total2_paths_equiv _ _ _)%weq.
    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂

HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
x₁: C₁
y₁: C₂
xy₁, xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
(weq_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat xy₁ xy₂
 ∘ weqtotal2
     (make_weq
        (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁))
        (HD₁ x₁ x₁ y₁ y₁ (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
           (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)))
     (is_univalent_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_help HD₂
        xy₁ xy₂)
 ∘ total2_paths_equiv
     (λ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)) xy₁ xy₂)%weq ~
idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)

p: transportf
  (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
  (idpath x₁)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
     (idpath y₁) xy₁) = xy₂
(weq_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat xy₁ xy₂
 ∘ weqtotal2
     (make_weq
        (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁))
        (HD₁ x₁ x₁ y₁ y₁ (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
           (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂)))
     (is_univalent_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_help HD₂
        xy₁ xy₂)
 ∘ total2_paths_equiv
     (λ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)) xy₁ xy₂)%weq
  p = idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁) p

(weq_iso_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat xy₁
   (transportf
      (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
      (idpath x₁)
      (transportf
         (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
         (idpath y₁) xy₁))
 ∘ weqtotal2
     (make_weq
        (idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁))
        (HD₁ x₁ x₁ y₁ y₁ (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
           (pr1 xy₁)
           (pr1
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₁,
                  sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
                 (idpath x₁)
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₂,
                     sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
                    (idpath y₁) xy₁)))))
     (is_univalent_sigma_of_twosided_disp_cat_help HD₂
        xy₁
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
           (idpath x₁)
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
              (idpath y₁) xy₁)))
 ∘ total2_paths_equiv
     (λ xy : D₁ x₁ y₁, D₂ (x₁,, y₁,, xy)) xy₁
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
        (idpath x₁)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
           (idpath y₁) xy₁)))%weq
  (idpath
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
        (idpath x₁)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
           (idpath y₁) xy₁))) =
idtoiso_twosided_disp (idpath x₁) (idpath y₁)
  (idpath
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁, sigma_twosided_disp_cat z y₁)
        (idpath x₁)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂, sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ z)
           (idpath y₁) xy₁)))

      apply idpath.

fg, fg': xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
transportf
  (λ x : pr1 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] pr1 xy₂,
   pr2 xy₁ -->[ f,, g,, x] pr2 xy₂)
  (HD₁ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g (pr1 fg)
     (pr1 fg')) (pr2 fg) = pr2 fg'
 apply HD₂.
  Qed.

x₁, x₂: C₁

f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧

Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
∑
fg : pr1 xy₂ -->[ inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)
     ][ inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)] pr1 xy₁,
pr2 xy₂ -->[
inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf),, inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg),, fg] 
pr2 xy₁

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
(λ fg : pr1 xy₂ -->[ inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)
        ][ inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)] pr1 xy₁,
 pr2 xy₂ -->[
 inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf),,
 inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg),, fg] pr2 xy₁)
  (let X := pr2 HD₁ in
   let X0 := pr1 X in
   let X1 :=
     λ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂) (xy₁ : D₁ x₁ y₁)
     (xy₂ : D₁ x₂ y₂) (f : C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
     (g : C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧) (Hf : is_z_isomorphism f)
     (Hg : is_z_isomorphism g)
     (fg : xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂),
     pr1 (X0 x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ xy₁ xy₂ f g Hf Hg fg) in
   X1 x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g Hf Hg
     (pr1 fg))

HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
pr2 xy₂ -->[
inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf),,
inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg),,
pr1
  ((pr12 HD₁) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g Hf
     Hg (pr1 fg))] pr2 xy₁

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
h:= make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
  (pr1 fg,,
   (pr12 HD₁) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g
     (pr2 (f,, Hf)) (pr2 (g,, Hg)) (pr1 fg)): z_iso (x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁) (x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂)
pr2 xy₂ -->[
inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf),,
inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg),,
pr1
  ((pr12 HD₁) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g Hf
     Hg (pr1 fg))] pr2 xy₁

        
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
xy₁: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₁ y₁
xy₂: sigma_twosided_disp_cat x₂ y₂
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
h:= make_z_iso_total_twosided_disp_cat D₁
  (pr1 fg,,
   (pr12 HD₁) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ (pr1 xy₁) (pr1 xy₂) f g
     (pr2 (f,, Hf)) (pr2 (g,, Hg)) (pr1 fg)): z_iso (x₁,, y₁,, pr1 xy₁) (x₂,, y₂,, pr1 xy₂)
pr2 xy₁ -->[ h] pr2 xy₂

        apply fg.
    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
is_univalent_twosided_disp_cat sigma_twosided_disp_cat
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
is_univalent_twosided_disp_cat D₁
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
is_univalent_disp D₂

      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
is_univalent_twosided_disp_cat D₁
 apply HD₁.
      
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: twosided_disp_cat C₁ C₂
D₂: disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category D₁)
HD₁: discrete_twosided_disp_cat D₁
HD₂: is_univalent_disp D₂
HD₃: locally_propositional D₂
HD₄: groupoidal_disp_cat D₂
is_univalent_disp D₂
 exact HD₂.
  Qed.
End DispCatOnTwoSidedDispCat.
